Fits the Oneplus perfectly and has all the cutouts lined up. The button feel is good, not too stiff but enough to keep them from accidentally being pressed when removing the phone from my pocket. There is one minor blemish at the bottom of the case, which looks like it may be from the molding process. The blue case is nice and dark, looks a bit more purple under fluorescent light than in the pictures but in sunlight seemed truer to the advertised color. All in all it's a well made case.<br>Update: Fits perfectly with the Orzly tempered glass screen protector I got. Please try again   </div></div></div> </span>    </div>            <div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R2CZSQOFY4BLK7" class="a-section"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary">19 of 22 people found the following review helpful</span><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="5.0 out of 5 stars" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R2CZSQOFY4BLK7/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/188-6240132-4176148?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00MC1O3P8&nodeID=2335752011&store=wireless"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R2CZSQOFY4BLK7/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/188-6240132-4176148?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00MC1O3P8&nodeID=2335752011&store=wireless"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">Feels Like a TPU but Looks Luxurious</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">         <span class="a-size-normal">     <span class="a-color-secondary">       By     </span>     <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/ARVTXTTEQKKK9/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/188-6240132-4176148" class="noTextDecoration">Robespierre</a>   </span> <span class="a-color-secondary"> on August 8, 2014</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R2CZSQOFY4BLK7" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Color Name: Matte Black<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">     Verified Purchase   </span>      <div class="a-section">   <span class="MHRHead">Just took delivery of two Diztronic cases -- one black, one red -- and tried both on. Here's a quick review:<br><br>At first glance, the Diztronic seems a simpler case than the Tudia. It has no hard plastic edges at all -- the case is made entirely of the same rubbery plastic -- but that's what makes it a true TPU bumper.  It's fitted to the OPO but could likely accommodate a thicker back cover if necessary.<br><br>The finish is matte all round.<br><br>Technically, this case might have been easier to manufacture than the Tudia. What makes it a much better case is the intelligent minimalism of the design and subtle detailing. The sides of the case are molded in a way that makes your OPO appear to be wearing a hard case. The flat carved side band looks like a mockup of the Spigen Neo Hybrid's "frame." It would be interesting to see what happened if the "frame" relief part of the case were a different color (so that the black case wore a red band, for example).<br><br>When you first take the Diztronic out of the wrapper, you only see the rubbery aspect, which makes it seem interchangeable with every other TPU. But after you put it on, the effect of the careful semi-smooth texture and matte color (which, as it does on Spigen and Urban Armor Gear's slate cases, glitters slightly), and especially the band-like cutouts on the sides of the device give you an unexpected sense of luxury. The slight glossy coating on the buttons gives them the effect of metal insets, all of which shows the thoughtfulness of the design.<br><br>I never thought that a molded rubbery TPU case could seem so different from the rest. Somehow, Diztronic managed to do just that. Great design team, great aesthetics, great details.<br><br>The black version is more deceptive than the red.</span><span class="a-declarative" data-action="columnbalancing-showfullreview" data-columnbalancing-showfullreview="{&quot;rest&quot;:&quot; Both versions are great, but get the black if you don&#39;t want people to recognize a TPU case when they see one.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;You&#39;ve won us over, Diztronic -- now make OPO owners even happier and create an Ultra case that will provide more drop protection!&quot;}"><a class="a-link-normal" class="a-letter-space"></span>Read more &rsaquo;</a></span> </div>  </div>             <a class="a-link-normal comment-link" title="2" Please try again   </div></div></div> </span>    </div>            <div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R5HZ8VWKMT5K4" class="a-section"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary">8 of 8 people found the following review helpful</span><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="5.0 out of 5 stars" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R5HZ8VWKMT5K4/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/188-6240132-4176148?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00MC1O3P8&nodeID=2335752011&store=wireless"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R5HZ8VWKMT5K4/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/188-6240132-4176148?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00MC1O3P8&nodeID=2335752011&store=wireless"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">Diztronic comes through again with a fantastic case for a fantastic phone</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">         <span class="a-size-normal">     <span class="a-color-secondary">       By     </span>     <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A33460JZ1Q0T25/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/188-6240132-4176148" class="noTextDecoration">P. Ranalli</a>   </span> <span class="a-declarative" data-action="cr-popup" data-cr-popup="{&quot;width&quot;:340,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;AmazonHelp&quot;,&quot;height&quot;:340}" style="display:inline;"></span><span class="a-color-secondary"> on August 17, 2014</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R5HZ8VWKMT5K4" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Color Name: Matte Black<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">     Verified Purchase   </span>      <div class="a-section">   I was lucky enough to get a OnePlus One, but because of the limited supply of them so far the case options are relatively limited.  I decided to wait for Diztronic's case because I have had their cases in the past for other phones and love them.  I am glad that I did.<br><br>This review will be simple.  This case fits perfectly on the OPO, including easy-to-use buttons and proper cut outs for all ports.  It fits well in your hand, has a nice feel similar to the back of the Moto X or Nexus 5.  I think it feels significantly better than the stock &#34;sandstone&#34; feel of the OPO.  It also comes up around the edges of the phone just enough to nicely protect the screen when the phone is face-down, but not so much as to be annoying or get in the way of the use of the phone.  It also helps &#34;even out&#34; the camera on the back, providing better protection for it as well.<br><br>All in all, I don't think you can ask more for a phone case.  It does its job of protecting the phone, while not adding any bulk worth noting and improving the feel and grip.  It provides all pros and no cons in my opinion and it is inexpensive to boot.  Diztronic comes through again with a fantastic case for a fantastic phone. </div>  </div>        <a class="a-link-normal comment-link" title="1"
